      <script>
        
        const transcriptButton = document.querySelector("#transcriptButton");
        
        transcriptButton.addEventListener("click", function() {
          const transcriptDiv = document.querySelector(".able-transcript-area");
          let expanded = this.getAttribute('aria-expanded')
              if (expanded === 'false') {
                this.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
                transcriptDiv.setAttribute("style", "display:block");
                transcriptButton.innerText = "Close Transcript";
              } else {
                this.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false')
                transcriptDiv.setAttribute("style", "display:none");
                transcriptButton.innerText = "View Transcript";
              }
        });
      </script>

    function navigateTo(id,type){
      if(type == 1){
      if(parseInt(id) != -1 && parseInt(id) != 0) window.location = "/casestudy_preview.php?id="+id;
      }else if(type == 2){
        //window.location = "/blog_preview.php?id="+id;
        window.location = "/blog/"+id;
      }
    }
